zeros_g_f32) * scales_g_f32\n                w_hi_deq = (w_hi - zeros_g_f32) * scales_g_f32\n\n                k_idx_lo = k_row - k_base\n                if k_idx_lo < BLOCK_K:\n                    x_lo = x_tile_f32[:, k_idx_lo]\n                    acc += x_lo[:, None] * w_lo_deq[None, :]\n\n                k_idx_hi = k_row + 1 - <content>
1: """Naive W4A16 weight-only quantized GEMM reference (correctness only).
2: 
3: AWQ/GPTQ-style scheme:
4:   x:      (M, K)               bf16
5:   w_q:    (K // 2, N)          uint8   -- two int4 weights packed per byte (low nibble = even-K, high = odd-K)
6:   scales: (K // group, N)      bf16
7:   zeros:  (K // group, N)      bf16    -- asymmetric (stored already as float zero-point)
8:   out:    (M, N)                bf16
9: 
10: Dequant (per group along K):
11:   w_bf[k, n] = (w_q[k, n] - zeros[k // group, n]) * scales[k // group, n]
12: where w_q[k, n] is the unpacked 4-bit value (0..15).
13: 
14: This reference unpacks to a full bf16 matrix and then runs torch.matmul. Slow and
15: memory-heavy on the dequant; the agent's solution must fuse unpack+GEMM.
16: """
17: from __future__ import annotations
18: 
19: import torch
20: import torch.nn as nn
21: 
22: OP_TYPE = "gemm_w4a16"
23: SUPPORTED_PRECISIONS = ["int4_bf16"]
24: HARDWARE_REQUIRED = ["RTX_PRO_6000", "H100", "B200"]
25: 
26: GROUP_SIZE = 128
27: 
28: 
29: def _pack_int4(w_q: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
30:     """Pack (K, N) uint8 in [0,15] into (K//2, N) uint8.
31: 
32:     Even rows go in the low nibble, odd rows in the high nibble.
33:     """
34:     K, N = w_q.shape
35:     assert K % 2 == 0
36:     lo = w_q[0::2].to(torch.uint8) & 0xF
37:     hi = w_q[1::2].to(torch.uint8) & 0xF
38:     return (lo | (hi << 4)).contig

m_start\n    actual_n = n_end - n_start\n\n    # Accumulators in FP32\n    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N), dtype=tl.float32)\n\n    # Pointers to current tile\n    x_tile_ptr = x_ptr + m_start * K\n    w_q_tile_ptr = w_q_ptr + n_start  # (K//2, N) - column-major-ish access\n    scales_tile_ptr = scales_ptr + n_start\n    zeros_tile_ptr = zeros_ptr + n_start\n    out_tile_ptr = out_ptr + m_start * N + n_start\n\n    # Loop over K in chunks of BLOCK_K\n    for k_base in range(0, K, BLOCK_K):\n        k_end = tl.minimum(k_base + BLOCK_K, K)\n        k_limit = k_end - k_base\n\n        # Load x tile: (BLOCK_M, BLOCK_K) bf16\n        # x is row-major: x[m, k]\n        x_tile = tl.zeros((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_K), dtype=tl.bfloat16)\n        for km in range(BLOCK_M):\n            m_idx = m_start + km\n            if m_idx < M:\n                x_row_ptr = x_ptr + m_idx * K + k_base\n                x_tile[km, :k_limit] = tl.load(x_row_ptr + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K), mask=tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K) < k_limit, other=0.0)\n\n        # Convert x to FP32 for accumulation\n        x_tile_f32 = x_tile.to(tl.float32)\n\n        # Process K in groups of GROUP_SIZE (128)\n        for g_base in range(k_base, k_end, GROUP_SIZE):\n            g_end = tl.minimum(g_base + GROUP_SIZE, k_end)\n            g_k_start = g_base - k_base\n            g_k_limit = g_end - g_base\n\n            # Group index\n            g_idx = g_base // GROUP_SIZE\n\n            # Load scales and zeros for this group: (BLOCK_N,) bf16\n            scales_g = tl.load(scales_tile_ptr + g_idx * N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N), mask=tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N) < actual_n, other=1.0)\n            zeros_g = tl.load(zeros_tile_ptr + g_idx * N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N), mask=tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N) < actual_n, other=0.0)\n\n            scales_g_f32 = scales_g.to(tl.float32)\n            zeros_g_f32 = zeros_g.to(tl.float32)\n\n            # Load packed weights for this group: (GROUP_SIZE//2, BLOCK_N) uint8\n            # w_q is (K//2, N), so row = g_base//2 + local_k\n            w_q_g_base_row = g_base // 2\n            w_q_g_rows = GROUP_SIZE // 2  # 64 rows for GROUP_SIZE=128\n\n            # Process each row in the group\n            for local_row in range(w_q_g_rows):\n                k_row = g_base + local_row * 2\n                if k_row >= k_end:\n                    break\n\n                # Load packed weight row: (BLOCK_N,) uint8\n                w_q_row_ptr = w_q_ptr + (w_q_g_base_row + local_row) * N + n_start\n                w_packed = tl.load(w_q_row_ptr + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N), mask=tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N) < actual_n, other=0)\n\n                # Unpack to two int4 values\n                w_lo, w_hi = _unpack_int4_to_fp32(w_packed)\n\n                # Dequantize\n                w_lo_deq = (w_lo - zeros_g_f32) * scales_g_f32\n                w_hi_deq = (w_hi - zeros_g_f32) * scales_g_f32\n\n                # Accumulate for even K row\n                k_idx_lo = k_row - k_base\n                if k_idx_lo < BLOCK_K:\n                    x_lo = x_tile_f32[:, k_idx_lo]\n                    acc += x_lo[:, None] * w_lo_deq[None, :]\n\n                # Accumulate for odd K row\n                k_idx_hi = k_row + 1 - k_base\n                if k_idx_hi < BLOCK_K:\n                    x_hi = x_tile_f32[:, k_idx_hi]\n                    acc += x_hi[:, None] * w_hi_deq[None, :]\n\n    # Write output\n    for km in range(actual_m):\n        out_row_ptr = out_tile_ptr + km * N\n        tl.store(out_row_ptr + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N), acc[km, :actual_n].to(tl.bfloat16), mask=tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N) < actual_n)\n\n\ndef _get_block_sizes(M: int, N: int, K: int) -> tuple[int, int, int]:\n    "', 'Select block sizes based on problem shape."', '\n    if M == 1:\n        # For M=1 (decode/GEMV), use larger BLOCK_N, smaller BLOCK_M\n        return 1, 256, 128\n    elif M <= 32:\n        return 32, 128, 128\n    else:\n        return 64, 128, 128\n\n\nclass Model(torch.nn.Module):\n    "', 'W4A16 GEMM: y = x @ dequant(w_q, scales, zeros)."', '\n\n    def __init__(self, M: int, N: int, K: int, group_size: int = 128):\n        super().__init__()\n        assert K % group_size == 0, "K must be divisible by group_size', 'assert K % 2 == 0, "K must be even (int4 packing)', 'self.M, self.N, self.K = M, N, K\n        self.group_size = group_size\n\n    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:\n        # Buffers are loaded from state_dict\n        w_q = self.w_q          # (K//2, N) uint8\n        scales = self.scales    # (K//128, N) bf16\n        zeros = self.zeros      # (K//128, N) bf16\n\n        M, K = x.shape\n        N = self.N\n\n        BLOCK_M, BLOCK_N, BLOCK_K = _get_block_sizes(M, N, K)\n\n        grid = (triton.cdiv(M, BLOCK_M), triton.cdiv(N, BLOCK_N))\n\n        out = torch.empty((M, N), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=x.device)\n\n        w4a16_gemm_kernel[grid](\n            x, w_q, scales, zeros, o

Must implement in solution.py with Model, get_inputs, get_init_inputs matching reference.py - Group size = 128 along K, asymmetric int4 with explicit zero-points and per-group bf16 scales - Inputs: x (M,K) bf16, w_q (K//2,N) uint8 (packed int4), scales (K//128,N) bf16, zeros (K//128,N) bf16 - Forbidden: bitsandbytes, marlin_kernel, torch.nn.functional.linear - Correctness tolerance: 0.10 abs/rel - Shapes: M=1 N=12288 K=4096, M=32 N=12288 K=4096, M=256 N=12288 K=4096, M=1 N=4096 K=4096, M=16 N=14336 K=4096 ## Progress ### Done -
